### [117] [Three-form dark energy: constraints and multi-probe comparison with $Λ$CDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27436)
*Mariam Bouhmadi-López,a Hsu-Wen Chiang,Carlos G. Boiza,Javier Ortega del Río,Thomas J. Broadhurst,Pisin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个具有高斯势的最小耦合三形式暗能量模型，利用多种宇宙学观测数据（CMB、DESI BAO、Pantheon+超新星、宇宙时钟、伽马暴）对其进行贝叶斯参数限制和模型比较。结果表明该模型能较好描述宇宙膨胀历史，在高张力数据组合下略优于ΛCDM，且展现出中间红移区的幽灵相特征，虽未显著缓解哈勃张力，但仍为ΛCDM提供了有物理动机的替代理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三形式场是源于高维理论、具有良好理论基础的暗能量候选者，具有丰富宇宙学现象学；当前宇宙学观测间存在张力（如H0张力），需探索超越ΛCDM的新物理框架。

Method: 构建最小耦合三形式暗能量模型（含高斯势），在贝叶斯MCMC框架下联合拟合CMB、DESI DR2 BAO、Pantheon+（含/不含SH0ES校准）、宇宙时钟及伽马暴数据；采用信息准则、贝叶斯证据及张力统计进行模型比较与评估。

Result: 三形式模型在CMB+BAO与Pantheon+SH0ES等高张力组合下轻微优于ΛCDM；在其他低张力组合或单类数据下与ΛCDM中性或略逊；重建出中间红移（z~1–2）的幽灵相（w<−1），两端趋近于宇宙常数行为；H0值可略升高但未显著缓解哈勃张力；整体与当前观测一致。

Conclusion: 三形式暗能量模型是一个可行且具竞争力的ΛCDM替代方案，其额外自由度有助于协调不同起源的宇宙学观测；其独特的动力学特征（如幽灵相）为未来巡天提供了可检验的预言。

Abstract: Three-form fields provide a theoretically well-motivated framework for dark energy, arising in higher-dimensional theories and exhibiting a rich cosmological phenomenology. We investigate a minimally coupled three-form dark energy model with a Gaussian potential and constrain it using current cosmological observations, including CMB shift parameters, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, Pantheon+ supernovae with and without SH0ES calibration, cosmic chronometers, and gamma-ray bursts. Parameter estimation is performed within a Bayesian Markov-chain Monte Carlo framework, while model comparison relies on several information criteria and the Bayesian evidence, as well as tension statistics. We find that the three-form model provides a viable and competitive description of the expansion history of the Universe. It is mildly preferred over $Λ$CDM for the combination of early and late-time datasets that are heavily tensioned (CMB+BAO and Pantheon+SH0ES). This preference decreases to neutrality for the other, less tensioned combination of early and late-time data, while for individual early-time or late-time datasets analysed separately, the information criteria are neutral or favour $Λ$CDM. This suggests that the additional degrees of freedom of the three-form field may help accommodate cosmological observations of different origins within a common framework. The reconstructed dark energy dynamics exhibit a characteristic phantom phase at intermediate redshifts while approaching a cosmological-constant-like behaviour at early and late times, providing a distinctive observational signature. Although the model does not significantly alleviate the Hubble tension despite allowing higher values of $H_0$, it remains consistent with current observations and offers a well-motivated alternative to $Λ$CDM whose predictions can be tested by future cosmological surveys.

</details>


### [118] [Simulation-Based Inference for Cluster Cosmology with Set-Based Neural Network Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27439)
*S. Zelmer,E. Bulbul,K. Lehman,S. Krippendorf,E. Artis,S. Grandis,N. Clerc,Z. Ding,L. Fiorino,V. Ghirardini,M. Kluge,N. Malavasi,A. Merloni,T. Mistele,K. Nandra,M. E. Ramos-Ceja,J. S. Sanders,F. Pacaud,A. von der Linden,J. Weller,X. Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于模拟的推理（SBI）框架，用于利用eROSITA全天空巡天（eRASS1）X射线星系团样本进行宇宙学参数估计，通过集合神经网络与掩码自回归流结合，直接利用完整星系团级信息，避免了传统方法中对观测量的压缩，实现了对Ω_m和σ_8的高精度约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: eROSITA巡天提供了前所未有的大样本X射线星系团数据，但要充分挖掘其宇宙学潜力，需构建能准确连接可观测量与宇宙学参数的稳健统计框架。

Method: 构建基于模拟的推理（SBI）框架：使用校准于eRASS1模拟的真实化星系团模拟生成流水线，通过巡天选择函数生成符合数据统计特性的模拟观测；采用集合上的图神经网络（GNN on sets）编码单个星系团信息，并耦合掩码自回归流进行灵活的后验密度估计。

Result: 框架在模拟测试中能准确恢复输入宇宙学参数，通过校准检验；对匹配eRASS1有效样本量（3259个星系团）的模拟样本，获得Ω_m精度11.5%、σ_8精度4.4%，精度媲美基于更大样本的传统MCMC分析。

Conclusion: 所提SBI框架无需依赖压缩的汇总统计量，可充分利用星系团级信息，具备鲁棒性与可扩展性，为下一代X射线星系团巡天的大尺度结构宇宙学分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: The unprecedented statistical power of galaxy cluster catalogs from the SRG (Spectrum Roentgen Gamma)/eROSITA All-Sky Survey provides a unique opportunity to place stringent constraints on cosmological models through measurements of structure growth. Fully exploiting the potential of these large X-ray-selected cluster samples, however, requires robust statistical frameworks that accurately connect observable quantities to the underlying cosmological parameters. We develop and implement a simulation-based inference (SBI) framework for cosmological parameter estimation using a realistic mock-generation pipeline calibrated on eRASS1 simulations. Synthetic galaxy cluster catalogs are propagated through the survey selection function to produce mock eRASS1 observations that reproduce the data's statistical properties. At the core of the method lies a set-based neural network (GNN on sets) that encodes information from individual clusters and is coupled to a masked autoregressive flow for flexible posterior density estimation. This approach enables the use of the full cluster-level information content without compressing the observables into binned summary statistics. Our framework recovers the input cosmologies within the inferred uncertainties, and passes calibration tests, demonstrating robustness in the presence of realistic survey effects. We obtain mock constraints of 11.5% on $Ω_m$ and 4.4% on $σ_8$ averaged over a suite of simulated cluster catalogs matching the effective sample size of the data set (3,259 clusters). We achieve a precision comparable to that obtained with traditional MCMC analyses based on substantially larger cluster samples. The framework is readily extensible to more complex forward models and additional observables. This work highlights the potential of SBI methods for next-generation large-scale structure analyses with forthcoming X-ray cluster surveys.

</details>


### [119] [Fast Radio Bursts as Cosmological Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27714)
*Manisha Caleb,Jéferson A. S. Fortunato,Steffen Hagstotz,Clancy W. James,Joscha N. Jahns-Schindler,Dylan Jow,Evan Keane,Koustav Konar,Yin-Zhe Ma,Daniele Michilli,Robert Reischke,Amit Seta,Priyanka Singh,Laura G. Spitler,Yidan Wang,Amanda Weltman,The SKA Transients SWG*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了快速射电暴（FRBs）作为独立宇宙学探针的潜力，重点分析其在测量宇宙膨胀率、检验等效原理、探测光子质量、追踪宇宙磁场及研究暗物质候选体等方面的应用，并基于SKA望远镜模拟FRB样本进行预测性研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FRBs具有高能量、强相干性和长距离传播特性，其传播过程中受色散、散射和法拉第旋转影响，使其成为探测宇宙重子分布、宇宙膨胀、磁场及基础物理效应的理想探针。

Method: 构建SKA望远镜可观测的合成FRB星表，结合FRB可观测量（如DM、散射时间、RM等），开展参数 forecasts，评估其对哈勃常数、等效原理、光子静止质量、宇宙磁场结构及暗物质模型的约束能力。

Result: SKA有望显著提升对宇宙膨胀历史的约束精度；可对等效原理偏差和光子质量给出比现有实验更严格的限制；能描绘大尺度宇宙磁场结构；并对轴子类暗物质等候选体提供新探测途径。

Conclusion: FRBs作为新兴多信使探针，在宇宙学与基础物理交叉领域具有独特优势，SKA时代将极大推动其科学产出，尤其在精确宇宙学和新物理探索方面。

Abstract: Fast radio bursts (FRBs) are brief, coherent radio pulses of extragalactic origin. They typically last from microseconds to milliseconds and have energies large enough to be visible over cosmological distances. Since FRBs interact with free electrons along their paths, the original burst is dispersed (Dispersion Measure, DM) and broadened (scattering). Furthermore, the burst's polarization is altered by Faraday rotation. Consequently, FRBs are excellent probes of the cosmological distribution of baryons, the expansion of the Universe, magnetic fields, and minuscule effects of fundamental physics that accumulate over vast distances. This chapter is the second of a trilogy of FRB chapters and discusses FRBs as a standalone probe. We first introduce the foundation of FRB observables related to those questions. Next, we lay the groundwork for forecasting SKA's potential by describing the method to simulate the expected FRB population observable with the SKA. These synthetic FRB catalogues are then used to investigate the SKA's potential to probe the Universe's expansion rate and fundamental physics, such as the equivalence principle and the existence of massive photons. Furthermore, we investigate the possibility of tracing cosmic magnetic fields and investigating different dark matter candidates.

</details>


### [120] [Inferring Cosmology and Astrophysics from the High-redshift 21cm Signal with SKA-Low](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27858)
*Anshuman Acharya,Satadru Bag,Sabrina Berger,Michele Bianco,Daniela Breitman,Lilian Crascall-Kennedy,Saswata Dasgupta,Abhirup Datta,Marian Douspis,Ivelin Georgiev,Sambit K. Method: 综述性分析：系统梳理用于预测21 cm信号的建模框架（解析、半数值、数值及模拟器）和用于连接观测统计量与物理参数的推断方法（贝叶斯、基于模拟、场级），并评估不同统计探针（功率谱、高阶统计、分布矩、形态学测量）对SKA-Low（特别是初始配置AA*）的约束能力。

Conclusion: 为实现SKA-Low在宇宙黎明与再电离时期的科学目标，必须协同使用多样化建模与先进统计推断方法，并整合多类统计探针，这是揭示早期宇宙物理性质的关键路径。

Abstract: The Square Kilometre Array's low frequency telescope (SKA-Low) will enable inference of astrophysical and cosmological parameters from the redshifted 21 cm signal, probing the Cosmic Dawn and Epoch of Reionisation. While the power spectrum is the primary target for initial detection, the inherently non-Gaussian nature of the 21 cm signal, driven by the patchy evolution of ionised regions and spin temperature fluctuations, encodes rich information accessible through higher-order statistics and morphological measurements. Extracting these constraints requires diverse inference tools, encompassing both sophisticated modelling frameworks (analytical, semi-numerical, numerical, and emulators) used to predict the 21 cm signal, and advanced inference techniques (Bayesian, simulation-based, field-level) to connect statistics to the underlying physics. This chapter reviews these tools and explores the constraining power of different statistical probes accessible with SKA-Low, including the power spectrum, statistics beyond order two, moments of the signal distribution, and morphological measures. Combining these complementary statistics is crucial for breaking parameter degeneracies and unveiling the properties of the early Universe. We specifically assess the potential of the initial SKA-Low configuration (AA*) to measure galaxy and IGM properties, demonstrating its capability for early science results. This chapter forms part of a comprehensive set detailing the Epoch of Reionisation and Cosmic Dawn science case for the SKA-Low telescope.

### [121] [A hidden reionization prior biases cosmological inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27903)
*Zihan Wang,Huanyuan Shan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文挑战了宇宙再电离是单一平滑过渡的假设，指出该假设与当前观测（如Planck光学深度、PkSZ限制和Lyα森林终点）存在张力；提出z≳12处存在早期再电离成分，从而放松中微子质量总和和σ₈的限制，并揭示再电离历史形状是宇宙学推断中未被明示的隐含先验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision cosmology assumes a single smooth reionization transition, but current observations (Planck optical depth, PkSZ limits, Lyα forest endpoint) cannot be simultaneously explained by any monotonic ionization history, indicating a need to revisit this assumption.

Method: The authors perform non-parametric reconstructions of the ionization history and use Planck EE polarization data to independently support an early ionization component at z ≳ 12; they then assess its impact on cosmological parameter inference, especially ∑m_ν and σ_8, via the A_s–τ_e degeneracy.

Result: Incorporating an early reionization phase relaxes the 95% CL upper bound on ∑m_ν to < 0.39 eV and shifts σ_8 toward values favored by weak-lensing surveys; these shifts stem from relaxing an implicit prior on reionization shape, not new physics.

Conclusion: The assumed shape of cosmic reionization acts as an unflagged systematic in cosmological inference; future CMB and 21 cm experiments will quantify this uncertainty, transforming it from a hidden bias into a statistical error.

Abstract: Precision cosmology assumes that cosmic reionization was a single smooth transition. We show that this assumption is in tension with current observations: the Planck optical depth, patchy kinetic Sunyaev--Zel'dovich (PkSZ)limits from SPT and ACT, and the Ly$α$ forest endpoint cannot be simultaneously reproduced by any viable monotonic ionization history. Non-parametric reconstructions and Planck EE polarization provide independent support for an additional ionization component at $z \gtrsim 12$. Incorporating this early phase relaxes the upper bound on the summed neutrino mass to $\sum m_ν< 0.39$~eV ($95\%$ CL) and shifts $σ_8$ toward values preferred by weak-lensing surveys, both consequences of the standard $A_s$--$τ_e$ degeneracy. These shifts arise from relaxing a hidden prior on reionization shape rather than from new physics, and identify reionization shape as an implicit prior in cosmological inference. Next generation of CMB and 21~cm experiments will be able to test this directly,which will convert what has been an unflagged systematic on $σ_8$ and $\sum m_ν$ into a quantified statistical uncertainty.

It arises from the interplay of the gravitational pull of dark matter and the expansion driven by dark energy. Major large-scale galaxy surveys map the distribution of matter and galaxies across most of the sky, spanning over 10 billion years of cosmic history. I will guide you through some of the principles and challenges behind predicting the statistical properties of the matter and galaxy distribution in vast cosmic volumes. ### [123] [UV artefacts in ultra-slow-roll models of inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28005)
*Gerald Barnert,Laura Iacconi,Hooshyar Assadullahi,Kazuya Koyama,David Wands*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了单场暴胀模型中，通过超慢滚等瞬态非吸引子相增强原初扰动以产生原初黑洞和标量诱导引力波的物理自洽性；发现解析Hubble流参数化隐含势能高阶导数的尖锐突变，需引入UV滤波来消除，并指出该简化参数化在非线性效应（如非高斯性）中可能不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验单场暴胀中基于Hubble流参数化建模瞬态非吸引子相（如超慢滚）的物理一致性，因其广泛用于原初黑洞与引力波研究但潜在理论缺陷未被充分评估。

Method: 通过重构标量场势能分析Hubble流参数化的隐含结构；识别高阶导数尖峰；提出基于离散傅里叶变换的UV滤波方法，在场空间中系统压制高频模式；检验Wands对偶不变性恢复情况。

Result: 即使缓慢的慢滚参数过渡也会在势能高阶导数中引入局域尖峰；UV滤波可有效消除Hubble流导出势中的尖锐特征；滤波后模型在超慢滚回退至慢滚过程中恢复Wands对偶不变性；未滤波模型可能在非线性可观测量（如非高斯性、圈图贡献）中引入虚假紫外效应。

Conclusion: 简单的解析Hubble流参数化在建模含瞬态非吸引子相的暴胀模型时缺乏稳健性，其隐含的紫外结构可能影响关键可观测量，需谨慎使用或辅以UV滤波等修正手段。

Abstract: Within single-field inflation, primordial black hole and scalar-induced gravitational wave production from enhanced primordial perturbations typically requires a transient non-attractor phase, such as ultra-slow roll. We investigate the physical consistency of modeling such scenarios through analytical Hubble-flow parametrisation. By reconstructing the underlying scalar field potential, we show that even slow transitions in the slow-roll parameters can hide sharp, localised spikes in higher-order derivatives of the potential at the transition from ultra-slow-roll to slow-roll. These are typically not found in analytic potentials. To evaluate the impact of these structures, we implement a UV-filtering procedure based on discrete Fourier transform to systematically suppress high frequency modes in field space in both classes of models. We find that the filter effectively removes sharp features in Hubble-flow-derived potentials. As a consequence, we show that UV-filtered models typically respect Wands duality invariance as the field evolves back from ultra-slow roll to slow roll. Beyond linear perturbation theory, the introduction of spurious UV effects might affect other observables, such as non-Gaussianity and loop contributions. Our results thereby question the robustness of simple analytical Hubble-flow parametrisation for modeling inflationary models with a transient non-attractor phase.

### [124] [Dark energy perturbations and the robustness of cosmological neutrino-mass constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28074)
*Yu-Hang Yang,Emmanuel N. Saridakis,Yi-Fu Cai,Hao-Ran Yu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了暗能量扰动对宇宙学中中微子质量限制的影响，发现忽略暗能量扰动会导致对中微子质量上限的误判；考虑其扰动后，中微子质量约束变得更严格甚至出现负值，表明中微子质量测量高度依赖于暗能量模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学观测对中微子质量总和的限制日益严格，接近振荡实验给出的下限，而动态暗能量模型被认为可能缓解这一张力，但以往工作常忽略暗能量扰动，动机在于检验该张力缓解是否稳健。

Method: 在动力学暗能量模型中一致纳入暗能量扰动，结合CMB、BAO、RSD和超新星观测数据进行参数估计与模型比对。

Result: 平滑暗能量显著放宽中微子质量限制，但允许暗能量聚集时，偏好更小甚至负的有效中微子质量；这种行为源于中微子自由流与暗能量扰动在结构增长观测量中的简并。

Conclusion: 宇宙学中微子质量测量本质上是模型依赖的，可靠推断必须一致处理暗能量扰动。

Abstract: Cosmological observations are placing increasingly stringent bounds on the sum of neutrino masses, approaching the lower limits implied by neutrino oscillation experiments. Recent studies have suggested that dynamical dark energy may alleviate this apparent tension. However, these conclusions generally rely on the assumption that dark energy remains smooth, neglecting its perturbations. In this work we investigate the robustness of cosmological neutrino-mass constraints by consistently incorporating dark-energy perturbations. Using CMB, BAO, RSD, and supernova data, we show that the commonly reported alleviation of the neutrino-mass tension in dynamical dark-energy models is not generic. While smooth dark energy substantially relaxes the neutrino-mass bounds, allowing dark energy to cluster shifts the preferred neutrino mass toward smaller, and even more negative, effective values. We demonstrate that this behavior originates from a degeneracy between neutrino free-streaming and dark-energy perturbations in structure-growth observables. Different combinations of neutrino mass and dark-energy clustering can provide similarly good fits to current data while yielding significantly different neutrino-mass constraints. Our results show that cosmological neutrino-mass measurements are inherently model dependent and that reliable neutrino-mass inference requires a consistent treatment of dark-energy perturbations.

### [125] [Thermal Sunyaev-Zel'dovich cross-correlations with unWISE galaxies: disentangling radio contamination, dust properties, and electron pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28099)
*Guandi Zhao,Alex Krolewski,Niayesh Afshordi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过在谐波空间中直接分析unWISE星系样本与Planck和ACT微波温度天图的交叉相关，同时拟合热SZ效应、宇宙红外背景（CIB）和射电辐射，发现包含射电污染的三组分模型显著优于忽略射电污染的模型；引入射电成分后，消除了先前观测到的负向星系–SZ交叉相关，得到正定且物理自洽的小尺度tSZ信号，并可用标准晕模型良好描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: tSZ与星系巡天的交叉相关是探测低质量晕中热气体的灵敏探针，但在关键角尺度上易受残余前景污染（尤其是射电辐射）影响，导致信号失真（如出现非物理的负相关）。

Method: 在谐波空间中联合拟合unWISE低红移星系样本与Planck PR4/ACT DR6多频段微波数据，构建含tSZ、CIB（含β₀、T₀参数）和幂律射电辐射（谱指数βᵣ）的三组分前景模型；利用Planck九频段进行模型选择，并将最优模型应用于ACT+Planck多频组合以获得洁净tSZ交叉功率谱。

Result: 射电成分被高显著性（9.5σ 和 11σ）检出；获得两组unWISE样本的CIB参数（β₀, T₀）和射电谱指数βᵣ；引入射电建模后，消除了ACT NILC重建中虚假的负交叉相关，得到正定tSZ–galaxy谱直至ℓ≈6000，且与Planck单独结果一致；该谱可由常规晕模型+广义NFW电子压轮廓良好拟合。

Conclusion: 射电前景污染是tSZ–星系交叉相关分析中不可忽略的关键系统误差源；显式建模射电辐射对获得可靠小尺度tSZ信号及准确推断星系周围热气体物理性质至关重要；所提方法为未来CMB-S4等高精度实验提供了稳健的前景处理范式。

Abstract: Cross-correlations between the thermal Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (tSZ) effect and galaxy surveys provide a sensitive probe of hot gas in low-mass halos, but on the angular scales of greatest astrophysical interest they are also highly vulnerable to residual foreground contamination. We analyze the cross-correlation of two low-redshift unWISE galaxy samples with Planck PR4 and ACT DR6 microwave temperature sky maps directly in harmonic space, fitting simultaneously for correlated tSZ, cosmic infrared background (CIB), and radio emission. Using the nine Planck bands to perform model selection, we find that a three-component model consisting of tSZ, radio emission, and a CIB amplitude term is strongly preferred over a model that omits radio contamination, with a significance of $9.5σ$ for the unWISE Low-z sample and $11σ$ for the unWISE Mid-z sample respectively. For the unWISE Low-z sample ($\bar{z}=0.14$) the preferred \textit{Planck} fit gives an effective CIB emissivity index $β_0=1.79\pm0.29$, an effective CIB dust temperature $T_0=22.0\pm5.1 K$, and a radio spectral index $β_r=-2.18\pm0.24$; for the unWISE Mid-z sample ($\bar{z}=0.23$) we find $β_0=1.41\pm0.13$, $T_0=28.0\pm4.2 K$, and $β_r=-2.62\pm0.26$. We apply this radio-inclusive recipe to the ACT+Planck 90, 150, and 220 GHz maps to obtain the best small-scale measurements. This removes the apparent negative galaxy-tSZ cross-correlation seen in the fiducial ACT DR6 NILC reconstruction and in no-radio fits. The cleaned tSZ cross unWISE spectra remain positive to $\ell \simeq 6000$ and are broadly consistent with the Planck-only reconstruction on overlapping scales. We show that these radio-cleaned spectra are well described by a conventional halo model calibrated to the galaxy population and a two-parameter generalized NFW electron pressure profile.

### [126] [The effect of dark energy on the void-halo perpendicular alignments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28151)
*Geonwoo Kang,Jounghun Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过AbacusSummit模拟套件分析了不同暗能量模型下空洞表面星系晕的形状取向，发现加速膨胀更快的宇宙中，这些晕更倾向于垂直于指向空洞中心的方向排列；该取向强度参数dt与暗能量状态方程参数w及wa呈双线性关系，表明该观测可作为探测暗能量动力学性质的独立探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用AbacusSummit中10种不同暗能量模型（含ΛCDM、wCDM和w0waCDM）的N体模拟数据，在z=0.1识别空洞及空洞表面星系晕，计算其形状主轴与指向空洞中心方向夹角余弦的概率密度p(cosθ)，并用基于微扰理论修正的单参数解析公式拟合，控制质量与球形度分布差异带来的伪信号。

Result: 发现空洞表面星系晕的垂直取向强度参数dt随暗能量压强更负、演化更快而增大；dt在w≠−1与w=−1情形间的差异可用关于w和wa的双线性模型精确描述。

Conclusion: 空洞表面星系晕的垂直取向是一种原理上可行、且有潜力的暗能量动力学独立探针。

Abstract: We report a numerical discovery that in a more rapidly accelerating spacetime, the galactic halos on void surfaces develop stronger perpendicular alignments with the directions toward the void centers. We utilize the halo catalogs from the AbacusSummit suite of simulations for $10$ different cosmologies that include one Planck $Λ$CDM, four $w$CDM and five $w_{0}w_{a}$CDM, which share the identical initial conditions except for the dark energy equation of state. For each cosmology, we identify the voids and void-surface galactic halos at $z=0.1$ and determine the probability density functions of the cosines of the angles, $p(\cosθ)$, between the shape axes of void-surface galactic halos and the directions toward the void centers. The numerically obtained $p(\cosθ)$ is fitted to an analytic single-parameter formula derived through an empirical modification of the linear perturbation theory. Eliminating spurious signals caused by the differences in the mass and sphericity distributions of void-surface galactic halos among different cosmologies, we detect a clear net effect of dark energy on the strengths of the perpendicular alignments of void-surface galactic halos, quantified by the single parameter, $d_{t}$. Noting that $d_{t}$ has higher values in the cosmologies where dark energy has more negative pressure and evolves more rapidly, we put forth a bilinear model for the difference in $d_{t}$ between the two cases of $w=-1$ and $w\ne -1$. Demonstrating that this bilinear relation excellently describes the numerical results, we conclude that the perpendicular alignments of void-surface galactic halos should in principle be a powerful independent indicator of the dynamic nature of dark energy.

### [127] [Searching for primordial features with radio surveys: synergy between the power spectrum and bispectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28172)
*Dionysios Karagiannis,Mario Ballardini,Roy Maartens*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合未来中性氢强度映射（HI IM）与宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测的综合预报框架，通过联合分析红移空间功率谱与三谱（bispectrum），显著提升对原初振荡特征的探测能力；结果表明，加入三谱可使振幅约束提升30–40%，并在多个情况下比功率谱本身提供更多信息，最终实现对原初特征频率的百分比级精度测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建联合HI强度映射（SKAO单口径、HIRAX干涉阵）与CMB的预报框架，联合建模红移空间功率谱与三谱，严格计入尺度依赖偏置、红移空间畸变及非高斯协方差；采用线性/对数振荡及尖锐物理模板进行参数拟合与误差预报。

Result: 三谱使振幅约束提升30–40%；在部分情形下三谱信息量超过功率谱；晚期引力贡献继承原初振荡结构，构成独立信息源；HI+CMB联合分析对特征频率达百分比级精度，优于纯CMB约束达75%（线性区）；非高斯协方差虽削弱三谱单独约束力55–90%，但联合仍具强优势。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive forecasting framework to assess the detection of primordial oscillatory features by exploiting the synergy between future neutral hydrogen (HI) intensity mapping (IM) surveys and cosmic microwave background (CMB) measurements. Focusing on next-generation single-dish (SKAO) and interferometric (HIRAX) radio configurations, we perform a joint analysis of the redshift-space power spectrum and bispectrum, consistently incorporating scale-dependent bias, redshift-space distortions, and non-Gaussian covariance. We investigate phenomenological templates with linear and logarithmic primordial oscillations, together with a physically motivated sharp-feature model. We find that including the large-scale structure bispectrum improves marginalised constraints on feature amplitudes by $30$--$40\%$ relative to the power spectrum alone and helps break parameter degeneracies. In several cases, the bispectrum contains more information on the power-spectrum feature parameters than the power spectrum itself. Much of this gain arises from the late-time gravitational contribution, which inherits the oscillatory structure of the primordial feature signal and acts as an independent source of information. While the CMB angular power spectrum is crucial for constraining low oscillation frequencies, joint interferometric IM analyses ($P+B$) outperform CMB amplitude constraints by up to $75\%$ in the linear regime. We also show that, despite non-Gaussian covariance degrading the independent constraining power of the bispectrum by $55$--$90\%$, the combined HI+CMB probe achieves percent-level precision on the frequency of primordial features, providing a powerful test of non-slow-roll inflation.

### [128] [HIcosmo: a differentiable JAX-based framework for cosmology inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28175)
*Jing-Zhao Qi,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了HIcosmo——一个基于JAX的高性能宇宙学推断开源框架，支持多种宇宙学模型和观测数据似然，利用自动微分和即时编译显著提升计算效率，并通过与Cobaya等工具对比验证其精度与速度优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应对第四阶段宇宙学巡天（如Euclid、LSST、DESI、SKA）产生的海量观测数据，亟需高效、可靠的宇宙学参数推断工具。

Method: 基于JAX构建端到端可微分宇宙学推断框架HIcosmo，涵盖前向建模、距离积分、似然计算、后验采样及Fisher预测；支持ΛCDM等暗能量模型及多种观测数据（SNe Ia、BAO、Planck、H₀、强引力透镜时延）；所有模块均使用JAX原语实现，梯度与Hessian由自动微分直接获得。

Result: HIcosmo与参考实现及Cobaya对比显示χ²差异为10⁻⁶–10⁻²，边缘化约束偏差小于0.2σ；CPU上采样吞吐量达Cobaya的8.7倍，GPU加速比最高达20倍；成功应用于多探针ΛCDM联合约束、暗能量状态方程限制及六种21 cm强度映射巡天的Fisher预测。

Conclusion: HIcosmo是一个高精度、高效率、可扩展的宇宙学推断框架，特别适合处理Stage IV巡天数据，在背景宇宙学参数估计中展现出显著性能优势。

Abstract: The Stage IV cosmological surveys, such as Euclid, LSST, DESI, and SKA, will deliver observational data of unprecedented volume, calling for efficient and reliable inference tools. This paper presents HIcosmo (High-performance Inference for Cosmology), an open-source JAX-based framework for cosmology inference. In HIcosmo, the forward model, distance integrals, likelihood evaluations, posterior sampling, and Fisher forecasts are all built from JAX primitives, so that gradients and Hessians of the log-likelihood are obtained directly by automatic differentiation, without any finite-difference approximation. The framework implements the $Λ$CDM, $w$CDM, $w_0 w_a$CDM, and interacting dark-energy models, and provides likelihoods for Type Ia supernovae (Pantheon+, DES-SN5YR, Union3), baryon acoustic oscillations (DESI DR1/DR2, SDSS), Planck 2018 distance priors, local $H_0$ measurements, and strong-lensing time delays. Its scope is restricted to background cosmology, with Boltzmann solvers and full perturbation-level likelihoods left to external tools. We validate HIcosmo against the reference implementation of each likelihood and against Cobaya. $χ^2$ values agree to absolute differences of $10^{-6}$-$10^{-2}$, and the marginalized constraints from the two codes differ by less than $0.2σ$ in every analysis tested. Leveraging just-in-time compilation and automatic differentiation, HIcosmo achieves about $8.7\times$ the end-to-end sampling throughput of Cobaya on CPU. As the dataset grows to survey scale, GPU acceleration over CPU reaches up to $20\times$. As applications, we present multi-probe $Λ$CDM joint constraints, dark-energy equation-of-state constraints, and Fisher forecasts for six 21 cm intensity-mapping surveys, including SKA1, MeerKAT, BINGO, Tianlai, and CHIME.

</details>


### [129] [Cancellation of one-loop time dependence in superhorizon curvature perturbations from all scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28247)
*Keisuke Inomata*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了在空间平坦规范下，超视界曲率扰动在一环水平上的守恒性，涵盖了所有尺度的环动量贡献，并通过δN形式考虑了非线性效应，消除了功率谱中虚假的时间依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往工作假设环动量k远大于功率谱特征波数q，忽略了k≲q区域；本文旨在克服该近似限制，全面分析超视界曲率扰动的一环守恒性。

Method: 采用δN形式处理非线性关系，严格计算包含所有尺度（尤其是k≲q）环动量贡献的一环曲率扰动功率谱，并统一计入边界项。

Result: 一环水平下超视界曲率扰动保持守恒：看似随时间演化的功率谱，在计入全部贡献（含边界项）后，其时间依赖性精确抵消。

Conclusion: 超视界曲率扰动的守恒性在一环量子修正下依然成立，且不依赖于k≫q的尺度分离假设，增强了暴胀宇宙学预言的稳健性。

Abstract: We show the conservation of the superhorizon curvature perturbations at one-loop level in spatially-flat gauge, including contributions from loop wavenumbers on all scales. In contrast to previous works, we do not assume a hierarchy $k \gg q$ between the wavenumber of the loop integral, $k$, and that of the power spectrum, $q$, and we explicitly include the regime $k \lesssim q$. Taking into account the nonlinear relation between the inflaton fluctuation and the curvature perturbation with the $δN$ formalism, we show that the apparent time dependence of the one-loop curvature power spectrum cancels once all contributions, including boundary terms, are combined consistently.

</details>


### [130] [Memoirs of the curvaton: non-perturbative non-Gaussianity and supermassive primordial black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28296)
*S. Allegrini,A. J. Iovino,G. Perna,H. Veermäe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了非二次势下的curvaton机制，通过构建局部非高斯映射ζ=F(ζ_G)，揭示了自相互作用如何影响curvaton振荡起始与有效状态方程，并导致新的非高斯性来源；结果表明自相互作用可增强或抑制非高斯性，强非高斯性甚至可压低功率谱；该机制为JWST观测到的‘小红点’提供了一种基于轴子类curvaton的原初超大质量黑洞种子形成新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准二次势curvaton模型难以解释强非高斯扰动，尤其在小尺度上；需拓展至更一般势能形式以探索非高斯性的新来源及其对原初结构形成的潜在影响。

Method: 采用缩略作用量（abbreviated action）方法连接冻结与振荡相，构建通用局部非高斯映射ζ=F(ζ_G)；系统分析二次、单项式、四次及余弦势下的curvaton动力学与非高斯性特征，并结合非微扰处理强非高斯情形。

Result: 发现curvaton自相互作用使振荡起始场依赖且改变有效状态方程，引入新非高斯性源；不同势下F(ζ_G)形式各异，非高斯性可被增强或抑制；强非高斯性可显著压低功率谱；提出A_pk∼10^{-5}的正强非高斯curvaton场景，兼容μ-畸变限制并可产生JWST‘小红点’对应的原初黑洞种子。

Conclusion: curvaton自相互作用是调控非高斯性的重要自由度，轴子类curvaton为实现强正非高斯性与原初超大质量黑洞种子提供了自然且可观测的框架。

Abstract: The curvaton provides a simple mechanism for generating strongly non-Gaussian curvature perturbations after inflation, with potentially important consequences on small scales. We study curvaton dynamics beyond the standard quadratic potential and construct the local non-Gaussian map $ζ=F(ζ_{\rm G})$ relating the curvature perturbation to an auxiliary Gaussian field $ζ_{\rm G}$. Curvaton self-interactions make the onset of oscillations field dependent and modify the effective equation of state once the curvaton enters the adiabatic regime. We incorporate these effects using the abbreviated action, which provides a compact way to connect the frozen and oscillatory regimes and exposes sources of non-Gaussianity absent in the purely quadratic case. We apply the formalism to quadratic, monomial, quartic, and cosine potentials, for which we derive the mapping $F(ζ_{\rm G})$ and show that self-interactions can either enhance or suppress the resulting non-Gaussianity depending on the potential and initial conditions. We consider non-perturbative aspects in the strongly non-Gaussian regime, and show how strong non-Gaussianity can suppress the power spectrum. As an application, we provide a bottom-up scenario in which strongly positive curvaton non-Gaussianity allows primordial supermassive black hole seeds at peak amplitudes $\mathcal{A}_{\rm pk}\sim10^{-5}$, which are compatible with the COBE/FIRAS $μ$-distortion bounds. This opens a new primordial scenario for the Little Red Dots observed by the JWST. The axion-like curvaton provides a particularly natural setting for this mechanism.

</details>


### [131] [First results of sub-arcsecond scale objects identified with ASKAP using interplanetary scintillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28302)
*R. Chhetri,J. S. Morgan,R. D. Ekers,E. M. Sadler,V. A. Moss,A. Waszewski,P. E. Gordon-Hall*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用ASKAP望远镜在823 MHz通过行星际闪烁（IPS）探测到131个致密射电源，并借助CRACO系统实现毫秒级采样，揭示了致密源的两类物理起源（喷流热点与核区AGN/CSO），并结合MWA低频数据确认其普遍具有峰谱型能谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索低频（<1 GHz）致密射电源的物理性质与分类，验证ASKAP开展IPS巡天的可行性，并弥补现有IPS观测在频率覆盖和分辨率上的不足。

Method: 使用ASKAP望远镜及CRACO数据捕获系统，在823 MHz进行全视场（35 deg²）IPS观测，以110 ms时间分辨率记录可见度数据；通过IPS调制指数分析识别致密源，并结合MWA在162 MHz的IPS数据构建谱指数。

Result: 检测到131个角尺度≲0.1″的致密源；明确区分两类源：嵌入延展瓣中的紧凑热斑 vs. IPS不可分辨的核区AGN或CSO；证实该样本在162–888 MHz普遍存在 peaked-spectrum SED。

Conclusion: 该试点研究验证了ASKAP+CRACO开展高时间分辨率IPS观测的有效性，为后续大规模IPS巡天奠定基础，并支持低频致密源以峰谱为主导的物理图景。

Abstract: We present a catalogue of 131 compact $(\lesssim 0.1 \,arcsec)$ sources detected at 823 MHz via their Interplanetary Scintillation (IPS). These measurements were made with the ASKAP telescope, across its full field of view of 35 square degrees, utilising all 36 Phased Array Feed (PAF) beams. To bypass ASKAP's standard correlator's minimum integration limit of 10 s, we used the CRAFT data capture system (CRACO), with visibilities sampled every 110 ms. Here we present the data processing steps, the sources detected, and their IPS-inferred properties. ASKAP IPS cleanly separates two populations: compact hot spots embedded in extended lobes and IPS-unresolved sources which are AGN or CSO sources associated with the galactic nucleus. We also compare these results with the results from observations of IPS at 162 MHz with the Murchison Widefield Array, providing the spectra of compact components between 162 MHz and 888 MHz. These measurements further re-enforce the dominance of peaked-spectrum SEDs in the compact-source population at frequencies below 1 GHz. This pilot study using test data is a pathfinder for a more comprehensive ASKAP IPS survey which is underway.

### [132] [Constraining primordial oscillations and inflationary particle production with Planck, ACT DR6, and DESI DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28310)
*Simran K. Nerval,Renee Hlozek,Hidde T. Jense,J. Richard Bond*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Planck 2018、ACT DR6和DESI DR2数据，结合pocoMC采样器，在多种振荡型原初功率谱模型（线性、对数及粒子产生诱导）中进行贝叶斯分析，结果表明：振荡幅度被严格限制在约2%的标量谱振幅As以内，粒子耦合常数g最大后验估计为0.034；尽管所有振荡模型拟合略优，但贝叶斯证据仍中等支持标准ΛCDM模型，未证实额外复杂性具有统计显著性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非标准暴胀模型常预言原初功率谱存在振荡特征，需用最新多源宇宙学数据对其进行严格检验与约束。

Method: 联合Planck 2018、ACT DR6和DESI DR2数据，采用集成pocoMC采样器的Cobaya框架进行贝叶斯参数估计与模型比较。

Result: 振荡振幅95%置信上限：A_lin < 0.021, A_log < 0.022, A_log_rf < 0.023（均≈2% As）；粒子产生模型中耦合常数g的最大后验值为0.034；所有振荡模型拟合略优于ΛCDM，但贝叶斯证据仅中等支持ΛCDM，对粒子产生模型无明确偏好。

Conclusion: 当前观测数据尚不足以支持引入振荡结构或粒子产生机制的非标准暴胀模型，ΛCDM仍是统计上最简且最受支持的基准模型。

Abstract: Non-standard inflationary models often predict oscillatory features in the primordial power spectrum. We present constraints on general oscillatory templates for primordial power spectra, including those that vary linearly and logarithmically with wavenumber, as well as oscillations induced by inflationary particle production. We utilize the Planck 2018 and Atacama Cosmology Telescope Data Release 6 cosmic microwave background data as well as large-scale structure data from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 2. To efficiently explore the multimodal posteriors for these models as well as performing mode comparisons, we integrate the preconditioned sequential Monte Carlo sampler, pocoMC, into the widely used sampling code, Cobaya. We find that the combined dataset tightens the 95% CL upper bounds on the general oscillation amplitudes to $A_{\text{lin}} < 0.021$, $A_{\text{log}} < 0.022$, and $A_{\text{log rf}} < 0.023$, restricting the amplitude to $\sim 2\%\, A_s$. For the inflationary particle production model, our analysis places a maximum a posteriori constraint on the coupling constant of $g = 0.034$. While these models all provide an improved fit to the data compared to the concordance $Λ$CDM model, the Bayesian evidence still reveals a moderate preference for $Λ$CDM compared to models with general oscillations and is inconclusive regarding the particle production model, suggesting that the added complexity of these models beyond the standard model is not statistically justified by current data.

### [133] [Superoscillatory initial states during inflation: theory, CMB constraints, and prospects for galaxy clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25133)
*Ali Nayeri*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个超振荡初态（SIS）在暴胀宇宙学中的显式边界作用实现，通过初始波泛函内带限量子干涉产生具有快速绕行相位的局域Bogoliubov激发，并据此推导出原初曲率谱、CMB功率谱投影及观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索初态量子干涉如何在宇宙学可观测量中留下可观测印记，为超振荡初态提供具体、可检验的物理实现框架。

Method: 基于初始时刻二次边界项构造超振荡初态，解析推导Bogoliubov系数与原初曲率谱；结合CAMB数值计算、CMB转移函数分析及星系巡天对比，评估特征信号在不同观测中的表现。

Result: 获得由超振荡参数(a,N)决定的局域振荡特征谱形；CMB中该特征被转移函数显著压制，Planck 2018数据给出λ ≲ 0.05的指示性限制；星系成团性比CMB更灵敏地保留完整振荡结构；同时给出偏振与三谱的关联预言及区别于一般激发态模型的结构判据。

Conclusion: 该工作为初态量子干涉影响宇宙学观测提供了首个自洽、可检验的理论框架，凸显星系尺度观测对探测超振荡初态的关键优势。

Abstract: We construct an explicit boundary-action realization of superoscillatory initial states (SIS) for inflation, in which quantum interference within a band-limited initial wavefunctional generates a spectrally localized Bogoliubov excitation with a rapidly winding phase. Starting from a quadratic boundary term on the initial time surface, we derive the Bogoliubov coefficients and the resulting primordial curvature spectrum, obtaining a localized oscillatory feature fixed by the superoscillatory parameters $(a,N)$ rather than imposed phenomenologically. We compute the projection of this feature onto CMB angular power spectra and show that transfer-function smearing strongly suppresses the oscillatory component; full CAMB calculations confirm the qualitative effect and show that a simple Gaussian approximation overestimates the peak signal by about a factor of three. Using Planck 2018 TT data, we obtain an indicative matched-filter bound $λ\lesssim 0.05$ for a representative feature centered near the first acoustic peak, $Δk/k_* = 0.05$ at $k_* = 1.45\times 10^{-2}\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. We further derive correlated predictions for polarization and the bispectrum, identify structural constraints that distinguish SIS from generic excited-state models, and show that galaxy clustering provides a qualitatively more powerful probe because it preserves the full oscillatory structure that CMB projection suppresses. This framework provides a concrete and testable realization of how initial-state quantum interference can imprint itself on cosmological observables.

</details>
